### [41] [Head-Aware Key-Value Compression for Efficient Autoregressive Image Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20600)
*Guotao Liang,Baoquan Zhang,Zhiyuan Wen,Yunming Ye*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出HeadKV：一种面向注意力头的KV缓存压缩方法，通过给不同注意力头分配异质预算与分层逐出策略，降低AR图像生成的显存占用并提高吞吐，同时保持图像质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AR视觉生成需要缓存全部已生成token的KV，导致显存高、吞吐低。已有工作用“仅保留少量缓存行”缓解，但对每个注意力头一刀切地分配固定预算，忽视不同头在感受野与关注范围上的差异，造成内存分配次优。

Method: 1) 观察：不同层/头展现不同的注意模式，有的偏局部，有的偏全局；同一层内同一头在不同token位置的模式基本一致。2) HeadKV：按头类型自适应分配KV缓存预算——对局部偏置头给小预算、对广域关注头给大预算；在生成早期识别头类型并在全程复用，无需额外训练或数据统计。3) 设计分层（Stratified）token逐出策略，优先保留长程依赖相关的信息。

Result: 在多种AR图像生成模型上进行大量实验，显示在显著降低内存与提升吞吐的同时，能维持图像质量；优于固定预算的缓存裁剪方法。

Conclusion: 利用注意力头异质性进行KV缓存压缩是有效且通用的。HeadKV在无需训练改动的前提下，通过早期头类型识别与分层逐出，达成更优的内存-速度-质量权衡，并可跨输入泛化。

Abstract: Autoregressive (AR) visual generation has achieved remarkable performance but suffers from high memory usage and low throughput, as it requires caching previously generated visual tokens. Recent research has shown that retaining only a few lines of cache tokens can maintain high-quality images while significantly reducing memory usage and improving throughput. However, these methods allocate a fixed budget to each attention head, overlooking the heterogeneity among attention heads, leading to suboptimal memory allocation. In this paper, we observe that attention heads across different layers exhibit diverse attention patterns, where some heads focus on local neighborhoods while others capture broader contextual dependencies. Based on this insight, we propose a novel head-aware key-value (KV) cache compression framework for autoregressive image generation, called HeadKV, which assigns smaller budgets to locality-biased heads and larger budgets to heads with broader attention. A key challenge lies in identifying the type of each attention head to guide cache compression. We further observe that, within the same layer, each head exhibits consistent attention patterns across token positions, \emph{i.e.}, a head's behavior for early tokens remains consistent with that for later tokens. This insight suggests that head types can be identified during the early stage and reused for KV compression throughout generation. Its advantage is that it requires no additional training or dataset-level statistics and generalizes seamlessly across different inputs. Moreover, we design a Stratified Token Eviction strategy to effectively preserve long-range information. Extensive experiments demonstrate its effectiveness across multiple autoregressive image generation models.

### [42] [Mind Your Margin and Boundary: Are Your Distilled Datasets Truly Robust?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20606)
*Muquan Li,Yingyi Ma,Yihong Huang,Hang Gou,Ke Qin,Ming Li,Yuan-Fang Li,Tao He*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出C^2R：结合“攻击感知课程学习+对比鲁棒目标”的鲁棒数据集蒸馏框架，在多数据集与多攻击下鲁棒精度平均提升2.8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据集蒸馏多仅优化干净精度，鲁棒性不可控；鲁棒DD虽有提升，但精度-鲁棒权衡差，原因在于：1）将所有对抗样本一视同仁，忽略鲁棒误差主要由鲁棒边距接近零的样本主导；2）未显式拉大全类间决边，攻击更易集中。

Method: 从鲁棒边距视角提出“扰动分数”近似每个样本的鲁棒hinge，构造优先关注最小边距对抗样本的课程；并行地引入类别均衡的对比鲁棒损失，强化对抗不变性，同时显式扩大跨类决策边界间隔。整体形成C^2R（Contrastive Curriculum for Robust DD）框架。

Result: 在CIFAR-10/100、Tiny-ImageNet与多个ImageNet-1K子集上，面对六种对抗攻击，C^2R取得最佳鲁棒精度，较既有鲁棒DD平均提升2.8%。

Conclusion: 面向鲁棒性的课程安排与对比目标相结合，可在数据集蒸馏中更有效地优化鲁棒边距与类间分离，从而在不牺牲过多干净精度的情况下显著提升鲁棒准确率。

Abstract: Dataset distillation (DD) compresses a large training set into a small synthetic set for efficient training, but most DD methods optimize only clean accuracy and leave robustness uncontrolled. Recent robust DD methods improve robustness, yet they often suffer from a poor accuracy-robustness trade-off because they (i) treat all adversarially perturbed examples uniformly, despite robust risk being dominated by near-zero robust margins, and (ii) do not explicitly increase inter-class separation in the decision boundary where attacks concentrate. We present Contrastive Curriculum for Robust Dataset Distillation (C$^2$R), a framework that couples an attack-aware curriculum with a contrastive robustness objective. From a robust-margin perspective, we derive a perturbation score that approximates each sample's robust hinge, enabling a curriculum that prioritizes the smallest-margin adversaries that most directly drive robust error. In parallel, a class-balanced contrastive robustness loss enforces adversarial invariance while explicitly widening boundary separation across classes. Experiments on CIFAR-10/100, Tiny-ImageNet, and multiple ImageNet-1K subsets under six attacks show that C$^2$R achieves the best robust accuracy, outperforming prior robust DD by $2.8$% on average.

### [43] [Beyond Routing: Characterising Expert Tuning and Representation in Vision Mixture-of-Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20610)
*Gene Tangtartharakul,Katherine R. Storrs*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文在视觉MoE中超越“路由看门人”的解释，直接刻画每个专家究竟编码了什么，发现主导性的“有生-无生”维度在门控到专家读出各层面稳定存在，但专家的调谐比类别更连续、跨越语义与视觉特征维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对MoE的解释多停留在路由统计（哪个类别去哪个专家），无法说明专家内部表征与调谐特性。作者动机是发展从专家层面与特征层面的分析方法，回答专家到底学了哪些视觉/语义维度、这种分工是否在不同随机初始化下稳定。

Method: 训练稀疏门控卷积式MoE，用对比学习目标在自然图像上学习；从门控层扩展到专家层：衡量每个专家的类别可分性与“最激发输入”来刻画调谐；从类别到特征层：用基于人类行为判断（THINGS）的语义维度解释调谐；并用调谐与表征相似性分析（RSA）评估跨随机初始化的专长分配稳定性。

Result: 1) 专家分工被强烈的有生-无生维度主导，从门控到读出一致；2) 该分工在独立训练中稳定复现；3) 路由显示稀疏类别偏好，但专家实际对连续的视觉与语义维度更宽广调谐，跨越类别边界；4) 不同专家的类别可分性相近，但其特征调谐各异。

Conclusion: 解释MoE应超越类别路由，关注专家层面精细调谐与表征结构；视觉MoE的专长是沿连续的视觉/语义维度组织，且存在稳健的有生-无生主轴。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models are often interpreted by analysing which categories are routed to which experts. However, routing alone does not reveal what each expert actually encodes. We train sparsely-gated convolutional MoE models with a contrastive objective on natural images and characterise expert specialisation using tools from visual neuroscience. Extending from gating-level to expert-level analyses, we measure per-expert category separability, and per-expert tuning using the most exciting inputs. Extending from category-level to feature-level explanations, we interpret tuning via semantic dimensions derived from a dataset of human behavioural judgements (THINGS). Finally, we use tuning and representational similarity analysis to assess the stability of expertise-allocation across independent initialisations. We find that an animate-inanimate distinction dominates expert partitioning, apparent from gating through to expert readout, and is stable across independently trained models. Although routing statistics suggest relatively sparse, categorical preferences, expert analyses reveal broader tuning to continuous visual and semantic dimensions that extend beyond category boundaries. Experts exhibit similar category-separability to one another, despite distinct feature tuning, demonstrating the explanatory benefits of moving beyond category-level analyses. Together, these results show that expert specialisation in vision MoEs extends well beyond category routing and is better understood by probing fine-grained expert-level tuning and representational structure.

</details>


### [44] [Accelerating Video Inverse Problem Solvers with Autoregressive Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20624)
*Taesung Kwon,Jonghyun Park,Hyungjin Chung,Jong Chul Ye*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AVIS 提出一种自回归视频扩散逆问题求解器，通过流式重建与更少的采样步显著降低首帧时延并提升吞吐，同时保持或提升重建质量；其加速版 AVIS Flash 仅在首块上施加测量一致性，将吞吐进一步提升至实时接近水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有零样本视频逆问题基于扩散模型虽能提供强先验，但存在两大部署瓶颈：1) 整体式视频复原导致首帧等待时间高；2) 为在像素域保持测量一致性需多次通过 VAE，吞吐低。需要一种既能降低初始延迟又能提高处理帧率的方法，以实现实时应用。

Method: 提出 Autoregressive Video Inverse problem Solver (AVIS)：利用自回归视频扩散模型按块/按时间步流式生成视频，天然降低启动延迟；以与观测一致的初始估计启动反向扩散，减少采样步数；并在采样过程中高效地施加测量一致性。提出 AVIS Flash 变体，仅在第一段视频块上强制测量一致性，后续依赖模型自回归传播以显著加速。

Result: 相较领先的非自回归求解器，AVIS 将初始延迟从 114s 降至 4s，吞吐从 0.71 提升至 1.18 FPS，同时重建质量更优。AVIS Flash 在单张 RTX 4090 上将吞吐提升至 5.91 FPS，性能仍具竞争力，效率-性能权衡更佳。

Conclusion: 自回归扩散与测量一致性初始化相结合，可在不牺牲交质的前提下显著降低延迟并提高吞吐；AVIS Flash 进一步表明只在首块约束一致性即可获得接近实时的速度，推动视频逆问题迈向实际部署。

Abstract: Diffusion models provide powerful priors for zero-shot video inverse problems, but their real-time deployment is hindered by two inefficiencies: high initial latency caused by holistic video restoration, and low throughput resulting from multiple VAE passes to enforce measurement consistency in pixel space. To overcome these limitations, we propose Autoregressive Video Inverse problem Solver (AVIS). The AVIS framework leverages autoregressive video diffusion models to restore videos in a streaming manner, naturally eliminating latency bottlenecks. Specifically, AVIS initializes reverse diffusion with a measurement-consistent estimate, reducing the required sampling steps. Compared to leading non-autoregressive solvers, AVIS drastically reduces initial latency from 114s to 4s and increases throughput from 0.71 to 1.18 FPS while achieving superior restoration quality. We further introduce a highly accelerated variant, dubbed AVIS Flash, that enforces measurement consistency solely on the first chunk. AVIS Flash substantially boosts throughput to 5.91 FPS on a single RTX 4090 GPU while maintaining competitive performance and achieving a favorable efficiency-performance trade-off, paving the way toward real-time deployment.

To address these problems, we propose LSENet, which builds upon the U-Net architecture by introducing three core innovative modules: To address vessel discontinuities, we introduce the Patch Information Enhance module (PIE), which replaces standard skip connections to execute patch-wise attention. To mitigate detail loss, the Multiscale Feature Fusion module (MFF) is proposed to feed the PIE module rich, multi-scale information by extracting visually interpretable features from both the original input and preceding layers. Finally, the Connectivity Refinement Decoder (CRD) is designed to refine features from all levels and utilize a large kernel in the final convolutional layer to reduce fragmentation. Experiments on three public datasets (OCTA-500, ROSE-1, and ROSSA) demonstrate that our proposed LSENet achieves state-of-the-art performance while requiring fewer parameters.

### [48] [RoPeSLR: 3D RoPE-driven Sparse-LowRank Attention for Efficient Diffusion Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20659)
*Yuxi Liu,Zekun Zhang,Yixiang Cai,Renjia Deng,Yutong He,Kun Yuan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出RoPeSLR：一种结合稀疏与低秩的注意力框架，在保持长距离相对位置信息的同时，将DiT的注意力复杂度降至次二次并在极端稀疏下保持性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DiT在视频生成上效果优异，但注意力O(L^2)限制了长序列推理。现有稀疏-线性混合注意力在极端稀疏下因RoPE在线性注意力中失去正交相对位置信息（“RoPE困境”）而显著退化，需要一种既高效又能保留3D相对位置结构的方法。

Method: 提出RoPeSLR：基于3D RoPE引导的Sparse-LowRank注意力。经验支撑下，将DiT注意力流形解耦为：高频“语义尖峰”稀疏集（O(L^{3/2})）与极低秩背景（O(d_h log L)）。用head-wise低秩参数化替代标准线性注意力，并注入可学习3D绝对位置编码以合成长程相对距离衰减，保证子二次稀疏度与子线性秩增长，适配超长视频。

Result: 在90%稀疏下，对Wan2.1-1.3B实现最高10× FLOPs降低；在HunyuanVideo-13B上对10万+ tokens序列推理达2.26×端到端加速；VBench质量几乎无损（平均下降<1.3%）。

Conclusion: RoPeSLR在保持3D相对位置信息与生成保真度的同时，大幅降低计算与加速超长序列视频生成，优于传统稀疏-线性混合注意力，具备良好可扩展性。

Abstract: Diffusion Transformers (DiTs) have revolutionized high-fidelity video generation, yet their $\mathcal{O}(L^2)$ attention complexity poses a formidable bottleneck for long-sequence synthesis. While recent sparse-linear attention hybrids aim to mitigate this, their performance severely degrades at extreme sparsity due to the "RoPE Dilemma": standard linear attention fails to preserve the orthogonal relative-position structure of 3D Rotary Position Embeddings (RoPE), neutralizing vital distance awareness. To address this, we propose \textbf{RoPeSLR}, a 3D RoPE-guided Sparse-LowRank attention framework. We establish that under empirically validated assumptions, the DiT attention manifold admits a decoupling into a high-frequency semantic spike set (bounded by $\mathcal{O}(L^{3/2})$ sparsity) and an extreme low-rank ($\mathcal{O}(d_h \log L)$) background continuum. Guided by this structural prior, RoPeSLR eschews standard linear attention for a head-wise low-rank parameterization equipped with a learnable 3D Absolute Positional Embedding (PE) injection, seamlessly synthesizing long-range relative distance decay. By guaranteeing sub-quadratic sparsity and sub-linear rank growth, RoPeSLR is exceptionally suited for scaling to ultra-long video inference. Extensive evaluations validate this scalable superiority: at 90\% sparsity, RoPeSLR achieves up to $10\times$ fewer FLOPs on Wan2.1-1.3B and delivers a $2.26\times$ end-to-end inference speedup on the ultra-long 100K+ token sequences of HunyuanVideo-13B, all while maintaining near-lossless generation fidelity (less than 1.3\% average VBench degradation).

To address this issue, we propose LER-YOLO, a reliability-aware sparse mixture-of-experts framework for misaligned RGB-infrared UAV detection. ### [50] [GSA-YOLO: A High-Efficiency Framework via Structured Sparsity and Adaptive Knowledge Distillation for Real-Time X-ray Security Inspection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20669)
*Jiahao Kong*

Main category: cs.CV

GSA-YOLO strategically integrates structured sparsity and adaptive knowledge transfer through three core components: Group Lasso (GL) applied to the network neck for robust feature extraction; Sparse Structure Selection (SSS) applied to the detection head for significant model slimming; and an Adaptive Knowledge Distillation (Ada-KD) mechanism for comprehensive accuracy recovery. *Mozhgan Nasr Azadani,Yimu Wang,Yongpeng Zhu,Lihong Chen,Milan Ganai,Sean Sedwards,Marco Pavone,Krzysztof Czarnecki*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VISTAQA提出同时评测多模态问答的答案正确性与像素级证据定位，并配套GROVE指标将两者以几何平均联合约束，揭示当前最强系统在“答对且证据对齐”上仍有明显差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前MLLM评测大多只关注文本答案或像素级定位之一，缺少对“推理-证据”一致性的强制约束，导致模型可能答对却未基于正确图像证据（或产生幻觉）。需要一个能同时衡量答案正确性与证据扎根的基准与指标。

Method: 构建VISTAQA基准：1,157条专家标注样本，覆盖6类任务与6个视觉领域，要求模型给出自由文本答案及与答案相对应的精确分割掩码；包含“无证据可用”的防幻觉样例。提出GROVE评价：对每个样本，将文本准确度与证据扎根质量通过几何平均联合，防止一方弥补另一方不足。

Result: 在多种具备grounding能力的模型与与通用MLLM的混合管线上实验显示：在GROVE度量下整体表现有限；存在明显的答案准确率与视觉证据对齐之间的性能鸿沟。

Conclusion: VISTAQA与GROVE为多模态推理中的“答案-证据”耦合评测提供了标准化框架；当前系统难以同时做到答对且依据正确视觉证据，提示未来研究需专注于提升可解释的证据扎根与防幻觉能力。

Abstract: Establishing a clear link between model predictions and the visual evidence that supports them is critical for transparency and reliability in multimodal reasoning, yet current multimodal large language model (MLLM) evaluations do not explicitly enforce this alignment. Existing benchmarks assess either textual answer correctness or pixel-level localization in isolation, leaving the coupling of reasoning and grounding an open challenge. We introduce VISTAQA, a comprehensive benchmark for joint evaluation of free-form answer correctness and pixel-level evidence grounding in visual question answering. VISTAQA comprises 1,157 expert-curated samples spanning six task types and six visual domains, ranging from direct perception to compositional and relational reasoning. VISTAQA requires models to not only answer correctly, but to also provide precise segmentation masks that support their answers. It also includes hallucination-aware examples where no valid visual evidence exists. To support this enhanced evaluation, we introduce GROVE, a unified evaluation metric that enforces joint correctness by combining textual accuracy and grounding quality via a per-sample geometric mean, ensuring neither dimension can compensate for deficiencies in the other. Comprehensive experiments across grounding-aware models and hybrid pipelines with general-purpose MLLMs reveal that even the strongest systems achieve limited performance under GROVE, highlighting a substantial gap between answer accuracy and visual evidence alignment.

</details>


### [52] [DarkShake-DVS: Event-based Human Action Recognition under Low-light andShaking Camera Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20680)
*Jiaqi Chen,Qinfu Xu,Liyuan Pan*

Result: 在三个数据集上进行广泛实验，EIS-HAR在各项指标上持续优于最先进方法，展现更强的稳健性与准确性，尤其在低光与强运动场景。

Conclusion: 结合事件相机与IMU，并通过非线性运动补偿与混合时空特征提取，可显著提升低光与6-DoF条件下的动作识别性能；新数据集为相关研究提供了标准化评测平台。

Abstract: Human Action Recognition (HAR) is a fundamental computer vision task with diverse real-world applications. Practical deployments often involve low-light environments and unconstrained 6-DoF camera motion, conditions that degrade visual quality, disrupt temporal coherence, and compromise reliability of existing methods. Event cameras, with high low-light sensitivity and microsecond-level temporal resolution, paired with an inertial measurement unit (IMU), present a promising solution. However, current research faces two key challenges: absence of a benchmark integrating low-light conditions, 6-DoF motion, and synchronized IMU data; and lack of effective motion compensation techniques. To address these, we propose Event-IMU Stabilized HAR (EIS-HAR), with two modules. The first is an EIS module that reduces motion blur via a non-linear warping function to reconstruct a motion-compensated input. The second is a HAR module with a four-stage hybrid architecture to efficiently extract spatiotemporal features for accurate action recognition. To alleviate data scarcity, we introduce DarkShake-DVS, the first large-scale event-based HAR benchmark that includes 18,041 realworld clips captured in low light and intense 6-DoF motion, supplemented by synchronized IMU data. Extensive experiments on three datasets demonstrate consistent superiority of EIS-HAR over state-of-the-art methods.

### [54] [Rethinking Cross-Layer Information Routing in Diffusion Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20708)
*Chao Xu,Maohua Li,Qirui Li,Yixuan Xu,Yanke Zhou,Yunhe Li,Cuifeng Shen,Hanlin Tang,Kan Liu,Tao Lan,Lin Qu,Shao-Qun Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Diffusion-Adaptive Routing（DAR）取代DiT中的传统残差相加，通过随时间步自适应地聚合跨层信息，显著改善训练稳定性与效率，并在ImageNet 256上显著降FID与加速收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管DiT在标记化、注意力、条件、目标与潜变量自编码器方面被广泛改进，但跨层信息在残差流中的传递仍沿用原始Transformer做法。作者观察到传统残差相加在扩散框架中出现三大问题：前向幅值单调膨胀、反向梯度急剧衰减、以及以块为单位的冗余，限制了训练效率与表示利用。

Method: 提出DAR：一种可学习、随扩散时间步自适应、且非增量（非简单逐步累加）的历史子层输出聚合机制，作为残差的替代。DAR可与现代Transformer增强方法（如REPA）兼容，实现对跨层信息的动态路由与加权；在训练与微调阶段均可启用。

Result: 在ImageNet 256×256上，DAR使SiT-XL/2的FID从9.67降至7.56（提升2.11），并以约8.75倍更少迭代达到基线的收敛质量；与REPA叠加后，早期训练加速约2倍。

Conclusion: 跨层信息路由是扩散建模中被低估的设计维度。DAR作为残差替代可稳定前向幅值、缓解梯度衰减、减少冗余，提升生成质量与训练效率；在大规模T2I模型的蒸馏微调中也能更好保留高频细节。

Abstract: Diffusion Transformers (DiTs) have become a de facto backbone of modern visual generation, and nearly every major axis of their design -- tokenization, attention, conditioning, objectives, and latent autoencoders -- has been extensively revisited. The residual stream that governs how information accumulates across layers, however, has been directly inherited from the original Transformer. In this paper, we present a systematic empirical analysis of cross-layer information flow in DiTs, jointly along depth and denoising timestep, and identify three concrete symptoms of traditional residual addition, namely monotonic forward magnitude inflation, sharp backward gradient decay, and pronounced block-wise redundancy. Motivated by this diagnosis, we propose Diffusion-Adaptive Routing (\textsc{DAR}), a drop-in residual replacement that performs \emph{learnable, timestep-adaptive, and non-incremental} aggregation over the history of sublayer outputs. Moreover, the proposed \textsc{DAR} is compatible with many modern Transformer enhancement methods, such as REPA. On ImageNet $256\times256$, \textsc{DAR} improves SiT-XL/2 by $2.11$ FID ($7.56$ vs.\ $9.67$) and matches the baseline's converged quality with $8.75\times$ fewer training iterations. Stacked on top of REPA, it yields a $2\times$ training acceleration in the early stage, suggesting cross-layer information routing as an underexplored design axis in diffusion modeling, one that operates orthogonally to existing representation-alignment objectives. Beyond pretraining, \textsc{DAR} can also be applied during the fine-tuning stage of large-scale T2I models and preserves high-frequency details during Distribution Matching Distillation.

### [55] [SAVER: Selective As-Needed Vision Evidence for Multimodal Information Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20713)
*Miaobo Hu,Shuhao Hu,Bokun Wang,Rui Chen,Xin Wang,Xiaobo Guo,Daren Zha,Jun Xiao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SAVER：在社媒多图场景下，先判断“是否需要看图、看哪些图”，再少量选图融合，从而更准确更省算力地做多模态实体识别与关系抽取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社媒帖子常附多张图，且与文本关系弱、冗余甚至误导。若始终进行多模态融合，会放大虚假视觉线索并浪费计算。关键是对每个候选跨度或实体对，决定是否需要视觉证据，以及从多图中挑选可信的小子集。

Method: 提出SAVER的“按需视觉”框架：1) 通过CGG（Conformal Groundability Gate）估计MNER中跨度级可“落地”性，并由两实体的可落地性推导MRE中的成对激活；在保留集上用类共形推断与Clopper–Pearson上界标定激活阈值以控制风险。2) 当被激活时，用次模（相关性-多样性）选择器从多张图中挑出紧凑证据子集；3) 采用Set Transformer聚合选中的视觉证据；4) 通过能量式联合打分头，融合文本、可选视觉证据、图文一致性与稀疏路由，实现实体类型判定或关系分类。

Result: 在多模态NER与RE上，相比强文本-only和“始终多模态”基线，SAVER稳定提升F1；同时降低AURC，提高在固定风险水平下的激活覆盖率，并减少FLOPs与P90时延。

Conclusion: 按需选择与可信子集聚合能在嘈杂多图社媒环境中兼顾精度与效率；SAVER提供受控风险的激活策略与高效证据选择，优于一刀切的多模态融合。

Abstract: Multimodal IE in social media is difficult because a post may attach multiple images that are weakly related, redundant, or even misleading with respect to the text. In this setting, always-on multimodal fusion wastes computation and can amplify spurious visual cues. The core challenge is to decide, for each candidate span or marked entity pair, whether vision should be consulted at all and, if so, which small subset of images provides trustworthy evidence.
  We propose SAVER, a selective vision-as-needed framework for multimodal named entity recognition and multimodal relation extraction. SAVER uses a Conformal Groundability Gate (CGG) to estimate span-level visual groundability in MNER, derive pair-level activation in MRE from the two marked entities, and calibrate the activation threshold on a held-out split via a conformal-style procedure with Clopper--Pearson upper bounds. When activated, a submodular relevance--diversity selector chooses a compact evidence subset across images, which is then aggregated by a Set Transformer. An energy-inspired joint scoring head combines text, optional visual evidence, text--image consistency, and sparse routing for entity typing or relation classification.
  Experiments show that SAVER consistently improves F1 over strong text-only and always-on multimodal baselines, while reducing AURC, increasing activation coverage at a fixed risk level, and lowering FLOPs and P90 latency.

</details>


### [56] [Holistic Reliability Propagation: Decoupling Annotation and Prediction for Robust Noisy-Label](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20725)
*Jingyang Mao,Ningkang Peng,Yanhui Gu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种在多媒体分类含噪标签下的“解耦可靠性”学习框架：分别为人工标签与伪标签估计独立的可靠性标量α与β，并通过整体可靠性传播（HRP）在输入/对比两分支中有针对性地使用，显著提升在合成与真实基准上的准确率，尤其在高噪声下仍具竞争力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通常将外部注释（人工/弱监督标签）与模型伪标签的可信度合并为一个权重，但两者出错机理不同（如人工标签系统性偏差 vs. 模型自训练误导），合并会掩盖差异，限制鲁棒性与优化效率。

Method: 用双层元学习为每个样本学习两个经批归一化的标量：α用于给定（外部）标签的可靠性，β用于伪标签的可靠性，二者不强制归一化或相加为1。提出HRP：1) 在输入/监督分支使用“可靠性感知的Mixup”并通过全局门控利用α；2) 在对比学习分支仅对伪标签为正的样本用β门控（beta-gated positives），从而分别路由两类可靠性到各自最合适的目标函数。

Result: 在合成与真实世界数据集上，相比强基线方法整体提升平均准确率；在极高噪声率场景下仍保持与最优方法相当的性能。

Conclusion: 将人工标签与伪标签的可靠性解耦并分别路由到匹配的训练目标，可在含噪多媒体分类中带来稳定而显著的收益；HRP提供了一种通用、鲁棒的训练范式，尤其在高噪声环境下依然有效。

Abstract: Learning with noisy labels in multimedia classification often combines external annotations and model predictions into a single reliability weight, even though the two sources can fail for different reasons. We instead estimate disentangled reliabilities: bilevel meta-learning produces two batch-normalized scalars per sample, alpha for the given label and beta for the pseudo-label, without constraining them to sum to one. Holistic Reliability Propagation (HRP) then routes them to different objectives, using reliability-aware Mixup with global gating on the input branch and beta-gated pseudo-label positives on the contrastive branch. On synthetic and real-world benchmarks, HRP improves average accuracy over strong baselines and remains competitive at the highest noise rates.

</details>


### [57] [GAMR: Geometric-Aware Manifold Regularization with Virtual Outlier Synthesis for Learning with Noisy Labels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20727)
*Ningkang Peng,Jingyang Mao,Xiaoqian Peng,Peirong Ma,Xichen Yang,Weiguang Qu,Yanhui Gu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种几何感知的流形正则化范式，通过主动合成虚拟离群样本、在类间构建能量屏障，缓解噪声标签下DNN过拟合并提升鲁棒性与OOD检测能力，且可即插即用，SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法多在受噪声污染的特征空间内被动筛样，本质难以区分“困难样本”和“噪声样本”，造成性能瓶颈。需要从源头重塑特征空间几何结构，以提升类内紧致与类间分离，从而更好地学习于噪声环境。

Method: 提出Geometry-aware Manifold Regularization（GMR）：主动合成虚拟离群样本，在数据流形之间显式构建能量屏障；施加几何约束促进类内紧致、类间分离；作为独立正则项与现有样本选择框架无缝集成，且对噪声模式无先验假设。

Result: 在CIFAR-10等多基准上超过SOTA，尤其在更具挑战的非对称噪声条件下优势显著；同时显著提升OOD检测性能与部署可靠性。

Conclusion: 主动重塑特征几何（通过虚拟离群与能量屏障）能有效区分困难与噪声样本，学到更鲁棒表示；方法通用、可插拔、对噪声分布无假设，并在分类与OOD检测上带来一致收益。

Abstract: Deep neural networks (DNNs) experience significant performance degradation when processing noisy labels, primarily due to overfitting on mislabeled data. Current mainstream approaches attempt to mitigate this issue by passively filtering clean samples during training. However, simple sample filtering within feature spaces degraded by noise struggles to distinguish between challenging samples and noisy samples, creating a bottleneck for model performance. We highlight for the first time the fundamental importance of actively reshaping feature space geometry for learning from noisy data. We propose a novel Geometry-aware Manifold Regularization Paradigm whose core idea is to explicitly construct energy barriers between data manifolds by actively synthesizing virtual outlier samples. By imposing geometric constraints that promote intra-class compactness and inter-class separation, this approach enhances the discriminability between hard and noisy samples, leading to the learning of more robust representations. Our regularization mechanism exhibits high universality, with effectiveness independent of any prior assumptions about noise patterns. It can be integrated as a standalone mechanism into existing sample selection frameworks, providing stronger robustness against diverse noisy environments. Experiments demonstrate that our paradigm achieves performance surpassing current state-of-the-art (SOTA) methods on multiple benchmarks, including CIFAR-10, with particularly pronounced advantages under more challenging asymmetric noise conditions. Furthermore, this paradigm significantly enhances the model's capability in Out-of-Distribution (OOD) detection, ensuring superior reliability and safety for deployment in open-world scenarios.

### [58] [Early High-Frequency Injection for Geometry-Sensitive OOD Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20728)
*Chuanjie Cheng,Ningkang Peng,Chenxi Liu,Yifan He,Peirong Ma,Yanhui Gu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出EIHF，一种在输入端强化高频信息的干预方法，无需改动训练目标即可提升后验式OOD检测的分离性；在CIFAR‑100与ImageNet‑100上提升FPR95与AUROC，但在Places场景迁移上受限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 后验式OOD检测依赖已学到的表示几何；作者通过频带分解发现低频输入导致ID/OOD特征差异弱，高频能强化可分性，因此希望在不改训练损失的前提下，让模型在早期看到更多高频证据以改善检测。

Method: 提出频带MMD^2诊断：对输入按频率分带，分别评估不同训练策略（CE、SimCLR、SupCon、PALM）下ID与OOD特征分布差异；据此设计EIHF，在第一层卷积前对输入进行高频增强/暴露（不改网络与目标），以重塑类条件特征几何并减少ID/OOD的马氏分数重叠。

Result: 在CIFAR‑100与ImageNet‑100上，EIHF对几何敏感的OOD检测器最有效；在一致的训练与打分设定下，EIHF降低ID/OOD马氏距离分数重叠，取得CIFAR‑100整体增益、在ImageNet‑100上平均FPR95最佳、平均AUROC次优；但在Places（以场景为中心的分布移位）上效果受限。

Conclusion: 高频输入成分对OOD分离性更关键；通过简单的输入端高频暴露即可在不改目标的情况下改善表示几何与OOD检测性能，但在场景型域移位上仍有局限，提示需结合语义/场景鲁棒性方法。

Abstract: Post-hoc OOD detectors score logits or features after training, so their success depends on the geometry already encoded in the representation. We revisit this assumption through a band-wise MMD^2 analysis across CE, SimCLR, SupCon, and the OOD-oriented representation method PALM. In our diagnostic, low-frequency input bands induce weaker ID/OOD feature discrepancy, whereas higher-frequency bands tend to provide stronger separability. This observation motivates EIHF, an input-side intervention that exposes high-frequency evidence before the first convolution without changing the training objective. EIHF is strongest for geometry-sensitive OOD detection: under matched training and scoring settings, it reshapes class-conditional feature geometry and reduces ID/OOD Mahalanobis score overlap. Experiments on CIFAR-100 and ImageNet-100 show gains on CIFAR-100 and the best average FPR95 with second-best average AUROC on ImageNet-100, while also revealing a limitation on the scene-centric Places shift. Code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/EIHF.

</details>


### [59] [TASTE: A Designer-Annotated Multi-Dimensional Preference Dataset for AI-Generated Graphic Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20731)
*Haonan Zhu,Elad Hirsch,Alexandria Minetti,Allison Nulty,Purvanshi Mehta*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出并发布一个针对平面设计评价的专业数据集 TASTE，并展示：设计师在多维标准上有一致信号；现有大模型评审在该任务上准确率有限；在该数据上训练的小头模型可显著提升与人类一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主流文生图模型与评审器多基于摄影风格的整体偏好标签，无法反映设计师在字体、层级、配色、版式、简报契合度等多维准则上的专业判断，导致监督信号粗糙、模型优化方向不明确。需要一个细粒度、面向平面设计的基准与分析框架。

Method: 1) 构建 TASTE 数据集：10 位专业设计师，针对 4 个 SOTA 文生图模型的输出，围绕 9 个设计准则在两个独立 cohort 上进行排序评估；每一准则约 1600 个评分，并附带整体偏好组的幻觉（hallucination）标记。2) 提出准则无关的信号检验框架：采用 Kendall’s tau、majority probability、Condorcet 循环，并与 p=4、R=5 的精确 iid-uniform 随机评审原假设比较，评估一致性与非随机性。3) 基准评测：比较 6 个开源权重 VLM 评审器（3B–33B）与 3 个专用 T2I 评分器（HPSv2.1、PickScore-v1、LAION-Aesthetic-V2），分析位置偏置与内容敏感性的权衡。4) 训练一个小型 pairwise-difference 头，在 TASTE 上进行学习并测试其与 5 人多数意见的一致性。

Result: - 所有 TASTE 准则均显著拒绝“随机评审者”原假设；设计师在平面设计上的一致性介于“食物/电影偏好”和“摄影风格图像质量”之间。- 现有评审器与评分器的宏观一致性最高不超过 0.55，且随规模增大主要在“位置偏置 vs 内容敏感”前沿上移动，并未带来准确度提升。- 基于 TASTE 训练的小型差分头达到 0.611 的一致性，约弥合至单评审上限 0.741 的一半差距。

Conclusion: TASTE 提供了面向平面设计、多准则、专家标注的强信号数据集与分析框架，证明专业设计维度存在稳定的非随机一致性；现有通用 VLM 与审美打分器难以可靠反映设计师判断；在该数据上训练的专用小模型可显著提升与人类评审的一致性，为改进文生图模型与评审器指明了多维监督与任务特化的方向。

Abstract: Text-to-image models produce graphic design at production scale, but their supervision comes from photo-style preference data with a single overall verdict per comparison. Designers evaluate along several distinct axes, including typography, visual hierarchy, color harmony, layout, and brief fidelity, and a single label collapses them. We release TASTE (Typography, Aesthetics, Spatial, Tone, Etc.): ten professional designers ranked outputs from four current text-to-image models on nine criteria across two disjoint cohorts, yielding 1,600 ratings per criterion plus per-image hallucination flags on the holistic-preference cohorts. We pair the dataset with three contributions. First, a criterion-agnostic signal test framework, using Kendall's tau, majority probability, and Condorcet cycles against exact iid-uniform nulls at p = 4 and R = 5, places designer agreement on graphic design between food and movie preferences and photo-style image quality, with every TASTE criterion rejecting the random-rater null. Second, no pre-trained system in our benchmark, including six open-weight VLM judges from 3B to 33B parameters and three dedicated T2I scorers, HPSv2.1, PickScore-v1, and LAION-Aesthetic-V2, exceeds 0.55 macro agreement with the 5-designer majority; VLM judges trade off position bias against content sensitivity, so scaling moves along this frontier without improving accuracy. Third, a small pairwise-difference head trained on TASTE reaches 0.611, closing roughly half the gap to the 0.741 single-rater ceiling.

### [60] [Deep Attention Reweighting: Post-Hoc Attention-Based Feature Aggregation in CNNs for Disentangling Core and Spurious Features under Spurious Correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20732)
*Kin Whye Chew,Jingxian Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文指出GAP导致核心与伪相关特征在空间维度被混合，限制了DFR的再加权效果；提出DAR以注意力方式在池化前对空间位置加权，能抑制伪特征、放大核心特征，跨数据集优于DFR。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CNN常利用数据中的伪相关，造成泛化与公平性问题。现有DFR仅在分类头重训，但其输入特征已被GAP空间聚合而相互纠缠，难以同时提升核心特征、压制伪特征，故需在聚合阶段实现可学习、可选择的抑制。

Method: 提出DAR：用可学习的注意力聚合模块替换GAP，并与分类头在目标数据上联合微调。DAR对每个空间位置（跨通道特征图）计算权重，实现自适应空间加权后再汇聚，避免把核心与伪特征无差别平均。

Result: 在多数据集、评价指标与消融实验中，DAR稳定超过DFR，显示注意力式聚合能减轻GAP导致的特征纠缠并降低模型对伪相关的依赖。

Conclusion: 后处理阶段若仅重训分类头不足，关键在于改造聚合机制。用DAR替代GAP并联合重训可在压缩前过滤伪特征，带来更好的鲁棒性与公平泛化表现。

Abstract: Convolutional Neural Networks (CNNs) often exploit spurious correlations in datasets, learning superficially predictive yet causally irrelevant features, leading to poor generalization and fairness issues. Deep Feature Reweighting (DFR) is a post-hoc technique that reduces a trained model's reliance on spurious correlations by retraining its classification head on a target dataset. However, we show that DFR is fundamentally constrained by operating on entangled features, limiting its ability to amplify the core features while simultaneously suppressing the spurious ones. We trace this entanglement to the ubiquitous Global Average Pooling (GAP) layer, which indiscriminately collapses spatially distinct core and spurious features into a single representation. To address this, we propose Deep Attention Reweighting (DAR), a post-hoc attention-based aggregation module that replaces GAP and is retrained jointly with the classification head. DAR computes an adaptive weighting of spatial locations across feature maps, enabling selective suppression of spurious features before the collapse into entangled features. Across various datasets, metrics, and ablations, DAR consistently outperforms DFR, demonstrating that our attention-based aggregation mitigates GAP-induced entanglement and reduces spurious reliance.

</details>


### [61] [Sketch2MinSurf: Vision-Language Guided Generation of Editable Minimal Surfaces from Hand-Drawn Sketches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20733)
*Wenda Wang,Anqi Liu,Junqi Yang,Lei He,Luying Wang,Jiachen Lu,Weixin Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Sketch2MinSurf：将手绘草图转为可编辑、拓扑一致的最小曲面3D几何；通过空间-拓扑编码与奖励调制的结构损失，实现平滑、无非流形伪影的可编辑流形，实验优于现有方法（拓扑相似度0.844）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GAN/NeRF/扩散等生成模型难以直接输出可编辑流形，且对非欧几里得曲面与拓扑一致性处理不足，影响设计工作流可用性。需要能从草图稳定生成拓扑可控、可编辑的3D曲面的方法。

Method: 混合视觉-语言与几何优化框架：1) 空间-拓扑编码，将几何表示为节点坐标与真实/虚拟边骨架元组，实现稳健拓扑控制；2) 结合最小曲面理论生成光滑曲面；3) 设计S2MS-Loss（结构损失），以奖励调制的目标共同约束几何重建与拓扑一致性；4) 以视觉-语言信号引导生成。

Result: 在100个草图测试集上，取得0.844的拓扑相似度，超越现有sketch-to-shape基线；生成的曲面是可编辑流形，且无非流形伪影；有高校公共艺术装置展示其人意图驱动的3D形态生成潜力；提供数据与代码。

Conclusion: Sketch2MinSurf通过空间-拓扑编码与最小曲面+视觉语言引导及S2MS-Loss，实现从草图到可编辑、拓扑一致的3D最小曲面生成，在定量与实际应用上均展示优势，适用于下游设计流程。

Abstract: Converting hand-drawn sketches into structured 3D geometries remains challenging due to the difficulty of representing non-Euclidean surfaces and maintaining topological consistency. Existing generative models such as GANs, NeRFs, and diffusion architectures often fail to produce editable manifolds directly usable in downstream design workflows. We present Sketch2MinSurf, a hybrid vision-language and geometric optimization framework that integrates vision-language guidance with minimal-surface theory to generate smooth and editable 3D surfaces from hand-drawn sketches. The core of our approach is a spatial-topological encoding that represents geometry as tuples of node coordinates and real/virtual edge skeletons, enabling stable topological control during generation. We further introduce the Sketch2MinSurf Structural Loss (S2MS-Loss), a reward-modulated objective that jointly constrains geometric reconstruction and topological coherence. On a test set of 100 sketches, Sketch2MinSurf achieves a topological similarity score of 0.844, outperforming existing sketch-to-shape baselines. The generated manifolds are directly editable and free from non-manifold artifacts. A public art installation at a university showcases the method's potential for human-intent-driven 3D form generation. The dataset and code are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Sketch2MinSurf/.

### [63] [Resolving Long-Tail Ambiguity in Unsupervised 3D Point Cloud Segmentation with Language Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20737)
*Siqi Wei,Hongbin Xu,Feng Xiao,Tian Lan,Chun Li,Ming Li,Qiuxia Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出LangTail：一种语言引导的层次化无监督3D点云分割框架，通过引入语言模型的均衡语义先验，缓解纯视觉聚类的长尾歧义，显著提升少数类表示与分割性能（在ScanNet-v2/S3DIS/nuScenes上分别提升+13.5/+12.9/+8.9 mIoU）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纯视觉的“以聚代学”无监督分割容易出现长尾问题：少数类特征被优势簇吞噬，导致表示和预测严重失衡。需要一种能为少数类提供均衡语义支持的机制，以避免聚类偏向头部类别。语言模型蕴含较为均衡的世界知识，或可作为外部先验弥补视觉偏置。

Method: 构建LangTail语言引导的层次化学习框架：1) 从语言模型提取实体级语义先验，获得跨类别、细粒度且相对均衡的知识表示；2) 将这些先验通过对比式对齐注入层次聚类流程，在多粒度层面建立语言–视觉关联；3) 以语言先验引导语义结构形成，防止少数类在聚类中被头部类吸收，学习对少数类更具判别性的表示。

Result: 在ScanNet-v2、S3DIS、nuScenes三个基准上，较现有无监督方法取得显著提升：mIoU分别提升+13.5、+12.9、+8.9。

Conclusion: 语言先验能有效缓解无监督3D点云分割中的长尾歧义，提升少数类表示与整体分割性能；LangTail验证了语言指导与层次聚类结合的有效性，并在多数据集上取得大幅领先。

Abstract: Existing approaches for unsupervised 3D point cloud segmentation predominantly rely on a purely visual similarity-based learning-by-clustering paradigm, which suffers from a fundamental limitation: long-tail ambiguity. In such a paradigm, features of minor classes are consistently absorbed by dominant clusters, leading to severely imbalanced predictions. To address this issue, we propose LangTail, a language-guided hierarchical learning framework that leverages the balanced world knowledge encoded in language models to mitigate long-tail ambiguity in unsupervised 3D segmentation. The key idea is to establish multi-level associations between language-derived semantic priors and visually underrepresented minor classes, thereby compensating for the biased attention of purely visual clustering toward dominant classes. Specifically, LangTail first constructs an entity-level semantic prior from language models, capturing balanced and fine-grained world knowledge across categories. These priors are injected into a hierarchical clustering framework via contrastive alignment. This guides multi-granularity semantic structure formation and prevents minor classes from being absorbed by dominant clusters, yielding more discriminative representations for underrepresented categories. Extensive experiments on ScanNet-v2, S3DIS, and nuScenes demonstrate that LangTail consistently outperforms existing methods by significant margins, \ie, +13.5, +12.9, and +8.9 mIoU, respectively. These results demonstrate the effectiveness of language priors in improving the representation of minority classes in 3D point clouds. The code will be released at: https://github.com/Whisky0129/langtail_official.

### [64] [STAR-IOD: Scale-decoupled Topology Alignment with Pseudo-label Refinement for Remote Sensing Incremental Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20738)
*Yaoteng Zhang,Qing Zhou,Junyu Gao,Qi Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出STAR-IOD用于遥感增量目标检测，通过结构拓扑蒸馏与聚类驱动伪标签缓解灾难性遗忘与漏标问题，在DIOR-IOD与DOTA-IOD上分别提升1.7%与2.1% mAP。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 遥感图像以流式到达，增量学习中传统检测器会遗忘旧类；遥感场景存在显著尺度变化与漏标，导致知识迁移与旧知识保持受损，以及旧类被误判为背景。

Method: 1) 子空间解耦拓扑蒸馏（STD）：对齐类别间拓扑关系，并在子空间中缓解由尺度变化引起的类内表示偏差，实现结构知识迁移与旧知识保持。2) 聚类驱动伪标签生成器（CPG）：基于K-Means自适应估计类别阈值，区分真阳性与背景，缓解旧类漏标；为即插即用模块。3) 构建两套RS-IOD数据集：DIOR-IOD与DOTA-IOD。

Result: 在DIOR-IOD与DOTA-IOD上分别较SOTA提升1.7%与2.1% mAP，兼顾基类与新类检测性能，并有效缓解灾难性遗忘。

Conclusion: STAR-IOD通过结构化蒸馏与聚类自适应阈值，面向遥感增量检测有效应对尺度变化与漏标问题，取得优于SOTA的均衡增量检测表现，并提供可复现实验与数据集。

Abstract: Remote sensing imagery typically arrives in the form of continuous data streams. Traditional detectors often forget previously learned categories when learning new ones; therefore, research on Remote Sensing Incremental Object Detection (RS-IOD) is of great significance. However, existing methods largely overlook the intra-class scale variations prevalent in remote sensing scenes, which undermines the effectiveness of knowledge transfer and old knowledge preservation. Moreover, RS-IOD also suffers from missing annotations, which cause the model to misclassify old-class instances as background. To address these challenges, we propose a novel framework, STAR-IOD. First, we introduce a Subspace-decoupled Topology Distillation (STD) module to transfer structural knowledge, explicitly aligning inter-class topological relationships and mitigating intra-class representation discrepancies induced by scale shifts. Furthermore, we introduce the Clustering-driven Pseudo-label Generator (CPG), a plug-and-play module that leverages K-Means clustering to dynamically identify class-specific thresholds, thereby guaranteeing an accurate distinction between true positive targets and background noise and alleviating the issue of missing annotations for old classes. We also constructed two Remote Sensing Incremental Object Detection datasets, DIOR-IOD and DOTA-IOD to facilitate research on RS-IOD. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method outperforms state-of-the-art approaches by 1.7% and 2.1% mAP on DIOR-IOD and DOTA-IOD, respectively, effectively alleviating catastrophic forgetting while preserving strong detection performance on both base and novel classes. The code and dataset are released at: https://github.com/zyt95579/STAR-IOD.

</details>


### [65] [Draw2Think: Harnessing Geometry Reasoning through Constraint Engine Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20743)
*Juncheng Hu,Jiawei Du,Xin Zhang,Joey Tianyi Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Draw2Think 让几何题的推理从“文本/代码内隐状态”变成“可执行、可校验的画布交互”。它把模型放进 GeoGebra 约束引擎的循环：提议-绘制-验证，确保每一步关系由代数约束严格满足，并把精确测量回填给模型，从而实现可审计的构建与测量。结果在多个基准上显著提高构建正确率与解题/渲染性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言模型在几何题上越来越准，但中间状态不可验证：文本推理或绘图代码并不保证真有满足约束的构型。基于渲染像素或一次性脚本的外化方法无法对每一步动作给出精确几何保证，缺少可审计性。需要把关系以代数定义强制执行，使推理过程落在可验证的共享画布上。

Method: 提出 Draw2Think：把几何推理重铸为与 GeoGebra 约束引擎的代理式交互。核心是 Propose-Draw-Verify 循环：模型提出构型假设；在引擎上逐步绘制并以代数约束强制关系；从画布获取精确测量与结构化观察；将其反馈给模型以继续推理。通过此外化，可分别审计两项属性：Construction Fidelity（画布是否实现了预期构型）与 Measurement Faithfulness（由约束得到的精确数值/关系）。

Result: 在 GeoGoal 上达到 95.9% 谓词级与 84.0% 严格题级构建通过率；在平面/立体基准上最高分别提升 4.1%/16.4% 的结果准确率；在 GenExam-math 上取得 68.2% 严格与 90.5% 宽松渲染得分。

Conclusion: 以代数约束驱动的可执行画布把几何推理的“内隐状态”转为可验证外化，带来可审计的构建与测量，并实证提升几何解题与渲染表现。该范式为几何推理提供了更可靠的人机共享工作空间。

Abstract: Vision-language models solve geometry problems with rising accuracy, yet their intermediate states remain latent and unverifiable: a relation expressed in textual reasoning or drawing code carries no guarantee that a constraint-satisfying configuration realizes it. We observe that existing externalization methods based on rendered pixels or one-shot scripts fail to provide exact, per-action geometric guarantees. Enforcing geometric relations by algebraic definition closes this gap: the workspace becomes a constraint-checked evolving canvas. We present Draw2Think, a framework that recasts geometric reasoning from latent spatial inference into agentic interaction with the GeoGebra constraint engine. In a Propose-Draw-Verify loop, Draw2Think externalizes hypotheses onto an executable canvas, measures exact geometric quantities, and feeds structured observations back to the model, so subsequent reasoning proceeds from checked canvas state grounded by the shared workspace. This externalization makes two properties separately auditable: model-level Construction Fidelity (whether the canvas realizes the intended configuration) and engine-level Measurement Faithfulness (exact values and relations from canvas constraints). Across construction, outcome, and rendering evaluations, Draw2Think builds canvases that pass 95.9% predicate-level and 84.0% strict problem-level construction checks on GeoGoal, improves outcome accuracy by up to 4.1%/16.4% on planar/solid benchmarks, and attains 68.2%/90.5% strict/relaxed rendering scores on GenExam-math. Project page is available at https://draw2think.github.io/

Crucially, heavy baselines like TotalSegmentator fail due to memory exhaustion on commodity hardware (Intel Core i5, 8GB RAM), our model performs robust inference, making it a viable solution for point-of-care diagnostics and deployment on edge platforms like the Nvidia Jetson Orin Nano.

Method: 1) 物理诱导标注：基于热辐射与热扩散的一致性，将单点标注经可微扩散模块扩展为可靠伪掩码；2) 双层双更新框架：在训练层优化检测器参数，同时由元分类器预测样本级损失权重以缓解不平衡；在超参/伪标层对扩散参数与伪标签进行梯度化更新，并利用检测反馈迭代精化，实现训练与超参联合自适应互动。

Abstract: Point supervision has become a scalable solution to address dense annotation for infrared small target detection, but its performance is limited by two coupled bottlenecks: unstable pseudo-label evolution in cluttered, low-contrast infrared imagery and severe sample-distribution imbalance. In this paper, we present a more adaptive and stable framework to address these issues. Leveraging the intrinsic consistency between thermal radiation patterns and heat diffusion, we propose a physics-induced annotation strategy that expands single-point labels into reliable pseudo-masks. To further enhance supervision and alleviate sample imbalance, we develop a bi-level dual-update framework that jointly optimizes detector weights, sample weights, and diffusion parameters. A meta-classifier dynamically predicts sample-wise loss weights, while a differentiable diffusion module refines pseudo-labels with detection feedback, enabling adaptive interaction between training and hyperparameter optimization. Extensive experiments across multiple datasets demonstrate five-fold annotation acceleration, superior detection accuracy, and comparable performance with 30% of the training data, validating the efficiency and practicality of our approach. ### [68] [VIHD: Visual Intervention-based Hallucination Detection for Medical Visual Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20772)
*Jiayi Chen,Benteng Ma,Zehui Liao,Winston Chong,Yasmeen George,Jianfei Cai*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出VIHD方法，通过针对性视觉token遮罩校准语义熵，用于检测医疗MLLM在VQA中的视觉幻觉，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医疗多模态大模型在辅助诊断中常产生看似合理但缺乏图像依据的幻觉，威胁临床安全。现有自省式检测多依赖启发式、与上下文无关的输入扰动，忽视解码过程中文本token与视觉token的细粒度依赖关系，导致检测不稳健。

Method: 提出VIHD，包括三步：1) 视觉依赖探测（VDP）：定位对视觉信息最敏感/占主导的解码层；2) 视觉干预解码（VID）：在这些层对与当前生成相关的视觉token进行有针对性的遮罩，促使语义分布对视觉证据变化更敏感；3) 校准语义熵（CSE）：比较干预前后的分布，量化校准后的语义熵，作为可靠的幻觉信号。

Result: 在三个医疗VQA基准、两种医疗MLLM上，VIHD在幻觉检测指标上稳定超过SOTA基线，验证了细粒度视觉依赖对检测效果的重要性。

Conclusion: 面向医疗MLLM的幻觉检测，利用视觉主导层与针对性视觉token遮罩来校准语义不确定性，可显著提升检测准确性；细粒度跨模态依赖建模是关键。

Abstract: While medical Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have shown promise in assisting diagnosis, they still frequently generate hallucinated responses that appear linguistically plausible but lack visual evidence. Such hallucinations pose risks to clinical decision-making and necessitate effective detection. Existing introspective detection methods primarily perform uncertainty estimation or logical verification by analyzing model responses conditioned on original or perturbed inputs. However, such external perturbations are often heuristic and context-agnostic, which overlooks the internal cross-modal dependency between generated tokens and related visual tokens during decoding. To address this issue, we propose VIHD, a Visual Intervention-based Hallucination Detection method that leverages targeted visual token masking to calibrate semantic entropy for more effective hallucination detection. VIHD locates visually dominant decoder layers via Visual Dependency Probing (VDP), executes Visual Intervention Decoding (VID) via token masking to calibrate the semantic distribution, and quantifies the resulting Calibrated Semantic Entropy (CSE) as a reliable hallucination signal. Extensive experiments on three medical VQA benchmarks with two medical MLLMs demonstrate that VIHD consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods, underscoring the importance of fine-grained visual dependency for hallucination detection. The code will be available at https://github.com/Jiayi-Chen-AU/VIHD

</details>


### [69] [AttriStory: Fine-grained Attribute Realization for Visual Storytelling with Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20777)

Result: 在多个现有故事生成基线中加入AttriLoss后，属性实现的指标一致提升，并保持与原有一致性机制兼容，展示了在细粒度属性控制方面的稳健收益。

Conclusion: 属性实现是视觉故事生成中独立且互补于角色一致性的重要维度。AttriStory基准与AttriLoss方法为细粒度属性可控的故事生成提供了有效路径，推动该领域向更精细的属性控制发展。

Abstract: Visual storytelling with diffusion models has made impressive strides in maintaining character consistency across narrative scenes. Towards this goal, we introduce AttriStory, a benchmark enabling attribute realization in visual storytelling. We curate 200 multi-scene stories across 10 distinct artistic styles using Large Language Model. Each scene is constructed with detailed attribute specifications to enable rich visual narratives. Further, to address attribute realization, we propose a plug-and-play latent optimization module that operates during early denoising steps, when the model establishes structural and semantic content. We achieve this through AttriLoss objective designed to maximize alignment between the cross-attention maps for desired attribute-object pairs while suppressing spurious associations, guiding models to localize attributes correctly. This approach operates orthogonally to existing consistency mechanisms, integrating seamlessly with current story generation pipelines without requiring architectural modifications. Our experiments demonstrate consistent improvements on incorporating AttriLoss across all baselines. This work positions attribute realization as a distinct, complementary dimension of visual storytelling, alongside character consistency, advancing the field toward fine-grained attribute-controlled story generation. Abstract: The rapid advancements in generative AI technologies, such as Stable Diffusion, DALL-E, and Midjourney, have significantly transformed the creation of synthetic visual content. The increasing realism of AI-generated images makes their detection a pressing concern for researchers, policymakers, and industry stakeholders.
  In this paper, we present the findings of the Defactify 4.0 workshop, which introduced the Counter Turing Test (CT2) for AI-Generated Image Detection. The competition consisted of two key tasks: (1) binary classification of images as either AI-generated or real and (2) identification of the specific generative model responsible for an AI-generated image. To facilitate this, we developed the MS COCOAI dataset, consisting of 50,000 synthetic images from multiple generative models alongside real-world images from the MS COCO dataset.

The results demonstrated that while AI-generated images can be detected with high accuracy (F1-score > 0.83), identifying the exact model used remains significantly more challenging (highest F1-score: 0.4986). ### [71] [What Semantics Survive the Connector? Diagnosing VLM-to-DiT Alignment in Video Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20795)
*Hangyu Lin,Chao Wen,Chengming Xu,Jianxiong Gao,Jiangning Zhang,Xiaobin Hu,Yanwei Fu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文质疑并实证：将VLM接到DiT前端并用连接器对齐会丢失细粒度结构语义，成为视频编辑中的主要瓶颈；提出TRACE-Edit数据集与诊断协议，系统评估多种设计并证明对齐非无损。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Flow matching based video generative models have been increasingly relying on prepended Vision-Language Models (VLMs) to handle complex, instruction-based video editing. However, we hypothesize that this alignment acts as a severe semantic bottleneck, degrading fine-grained structural variables. Verifying this is challenging, as end-to-end evaluations conflate alignment failures with generation errors, and natural datasets lack disentangled annotations. To rigorously investigate this, we propose a controlled data processing pipeline based on video composition that results in TRACE-Edit, a diagnostic dataset focusing on relation-based editing. Leveraging this dataset, we propose a comprehensive diagnostic protocol to analyze two important designs of meta-query and connector in the existing video editing models. Systematic evaluation of four representative model cases reveals that fine-grained structural semantics can be severely degraded during alignment. Our findings overturn the assumption of lossless semantic transfer, identifying the VLM-to-DiT alignment as a major bottleneck and providing a new diagnostic foundation for future multi-modal alignment architectures.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有将基础视觉模型（SAM/DINO）先验蒸馏进LDM的表示对齐方法在极高分辨率时失效：直接补丁级对齐会扰动预训练潜在流形，导致生成质量退化，形成“学得上去但画崩”的矛盾，需要一种既利用强先验又不破坏原生生成能力的对齐机制。

Method: 提出SGA：不做逐点/逐补丁强配准，而是对齐生成特征与先验特征的空间自相似（Gram矩阵）分布，作为“非侵入式”约束，建立宏观结构一致性；同时保留原生LDM训练/采样目标以维持像素级细节。该策略可无缝施加于扩散过程中的中间特征及VAE潜表示。

Result: 在超高分辨率文本生成任务上，SGA相较现有表示对齐方法取得SOTA：全局结构更稳、细节更锐，且未牺牲原模型的生成保真；广泛实验验证其在多层位点（扩散特征与VAE潜空间）上的通用性与有效性。

Conclusion: 通过对齐空间自相似而非直接特征，SGA在不扰动潜在流形的前提下引入强先验，实现全局结构与微观细节的和解，为超高分辨率LDM提供通用、可插拔的对齐框架。

Abstract: Modern ultra-high-resolution image synthesis relies heavily on the robust generative capacity of large-scale pre-trained Latent Diffusion Models (LDMs). While recent representation alignment methods have proven effective by distilling visual priors from foundation models (e.g., SAM or DINO) into generative latent features, scaling these approaches to pre-trained LDMs at extreme resolutions exposes a critical learnability-fidelity conflict. Specifically, forcing direct patch-wise feature distillation inherently perturbs the pre-trained latent manifold, ultimately leading to generation degradation. To address this bottleneck, we propose Spatial Gram Alignment (SGA), a novel framework that explicitly leverages the representation priors of vision foundation models while preserving the native generative capacity of LDMs. Moving beyond restrictive direct alignment, SGA imposes a non-invasive spatial constraint by aligning the internal self-similarities of the generative features with those of the foundation priors. This spatial constraint effectively establishes macroscopic structural coherence, while the native generative objectives retain the microscopic pixel-level fidelity inherent to the original LDMs. Notably, this versatile strategy integrates seamlessly across both intermediate diffusion features and VAE latents within pre-trained LDMs. Extensive experiments demonstrate that SGA achieves state-of-the-art performance for ultra-high-resolution text-to-image synthesis, yielding an effective reconciliation between global structural integrity and fine-grained visual details. Code is available at https://github.com/zhang0jhon/SGA.

</details>


### [75] [OSGNet with MLLM Reranking @ Ego4D Episodic Memory Challenge 2026](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20818)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长时、未裁剪的第一人称视频中进行精确的自然语言驱动时间片段定位很难；传统管线召回高但语义推理弱，MLLM推理强但端到端效率与稳定性不足。需要一种方法既保留候选召回与效率，又引入MLLM的强语义对齐能力。

Method: 两阶段重排序：1）用现有定位模型OSGNet对长视频产生候选时间段；2）将候选及文本查询输入MLLM进行跨模态语义匹配，选择最佳片段作为最终预测。核心是将MLLM作为轻量重排器而非端到端定位器，提升精度且控制成本。

Result: 在Ego4D Episodic Memory Challenge 2026的Natural Language Queries与GoalStep赛道均获第一名，显示在长视频语言定位任务上的显著性能优势。

Conclusion: 将MLLM以重排序组件集成到传统定位流水线中，能在不牺牲效率与召回的前提下大幅提升语义匹配与最终定位精度；该策略通用且可复用，代码已开源。

Abstract: In this report, we present our champion solutions for the Natural Language Queries and GoalStep tracks of the Ego4D Episodic Memory Challenge at CVPR 2026. Both tracks require accurately localizing temporal segments from long untrimmed egocentric videos. To address these tasks, we propose a reranking-based framework that effectively leverages the strong video-language reasoning capability of multimodal large language model (MLLM) while preserving the efficiency and candidate recall of conventional localization pipelines. Specifically, we first obtain a set of candidate segments from existing localization model OSGNet, and then employ MLLM to select the segment that best matches the given query, thereby refining the final prediction. Ultimately, our method achieved first place in both the Natural Language Queries and GoalStep tracks. Our code can be found at https://github.com/iLearn-Lab/CVPR25-OSGNet.

### [76] [AIR: Amortized Image Reconstruction Framework for Self-Supervised Feed-Forward 2D Gaussian Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20820)
*Zhaojie Zeng,Yuesong Wang,Yawei Luo,Tao Guan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AIR是一种自监督前馈式框架，将传统逐图像的高斯拟合优化“摊销”为一次网络前向，从而免去测试时优化；通过分阶段残差架构与显式阶段控制，逐步在欠重建区域添加2D高斯基元，并用“预测-优化-蒸馏”训练稳定多阶段预测，最后跨阶段联合微调并引入自适应量化以紧凑存储；在Kodak与DIV2K上，较代表性高斯基方法更高画质且编码时间仅160–300ms。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有2D高斯splatting图像重建需要每幅图像进行代价高的迭代优化，或依赖手工规则分配基元，限制了效率与泛化。作者希望在保持或提升重建质量的同时，消除测试时优化开销，并自动、数据驱动地分配高斯基元，实现快速高质量与紧凑存储。

Method: 1) 前馈“摊销”网络：将高斯拟合从逐图像迭代转为一次网络预测。2) 分阶段残差架构：从粗到细逐阶段预测新的高斯，显式在残差上工作。3) 阶段控制（Stage Control）：仅在欠重建区域激活新增基元，抑制冗余与溢出。4) 预测–优化–蒸馏：先用短步优化得到高斯增量，再把其知识蒸馏回预测器，稳定多阶段训练。5) 跨阶段联合微调与图像自适应量化：进一步提升质量并降低存储开销。

Result: 在Kodak与DIV2K数据集上，相较代表性高斯基重建基线，AIR在画质指标上更优，同时大幅降低编码时间至约160–300毫秒；并能以自适应量化实现紧凑的高斯参数存储。

Conclusion: AIR证明了用自监督前馈网络可有效“摊销”高斯拟合，结合阶段式残差与显式控制、以及预测–优化–蒸馏训练策略，在无需测试时优化的前提下实现更优的重建质量、显著更快的编码速度与更紧凑的表示。

Abstract: 2D Gaussian splatting provides an efficient explicit representation for image reconstruction, but existing methods still require costly per-image iterative optimization or rely on handcrafted priors for primitive allocation. We present AIR, a self-supervised feed-forward framework that amortizes iterative Gaussian fitting into a single network pass, eliminating per-image test-time optimization. AIR adopts a stage-wise residual architecture that progressively predicts additional Gaussian primitives from reconstruction residuals, together with an explicit Stage Control mechanism that activates new primitives only in under-reconstructed regions. A Predict--Optimize--Distill training strategy stabilizes multi-stage prediction by distilling short-horizon optimized Gaussian increments back into the predictor. The stabilized predictor is then jointly finetuned across stages and equipped with an image-adaptive quantizer for compact Gaussian storage. Experiments on Kodak and DIV2K show that AIR achieves better reconstruction quality than representative Gaussian-based baselines while reducing encoding time to 160--300\,ms. Code: https://github.com/whoiszzj/AIR.git

</details>


### [77] [VSCD: Video-based Scene Change Detection in Unaligned Scenes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20821)
*Jiae Yoon,Ue-Hwan Kim*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 任务定义：输入参考与查询视频（不同时间、不同相机轨迹、不同步），输出每个查询帧的像素级变化掩码。2) 数据：超过110万帧，像素精确变化标注，另有真实域测试集评估跨域迁移。3) 模型：查询中心的多参考架构；仅用变化掩码监督来隐式学习时序匹配；通过局部补丁对应将候选参考特征对齐到查询；在帧级与补丁级进行置信度加权融合候选变化特征；一次性高分辨率解码每帧掩码。

Abstract: Detecting what has changed in an environment is essential for long-term autonomy, yet most change detection settings assume fixed viewpoints, mild misalignment, or only a few changed objects. We introduce Video-based Scene Change Detection (VSCD), which predicts a pixel-wise change mask for each query frame, given a reference and a query RGB video of the same indoor space recorded at different times under unconstrained camera motion. The two videos are not temporally synchronized, and many object instances may appear or disappear. To study this setting, we build a large-scale benchmark with over 1.1 million frames annotated with pixel-accurate change masks, together with a real-world test set for evaluating transfer beyond simulation. We propose a query-centric multi-reference model that learns temporal matching implicitly from change-mask supervision, aligns candidate reference features to the query via local patch correspondence, and fuses per-candidate change features using frame-level and patch-level confidence before decoding a high-resolution mask once per frame. Our approach achieves state-of-the-art performance against strong image- and video-based baselines, and we validate its real-world impact by deploying it on a mobile robot for two downstream applications -- visual surveillance and object incremental learning.

### [78] [TERDNet: Transformer Encoder-Recurrent Decoder Network for Scene Change Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20822)
*Jiae Yoon,Ue-Hwan Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出TERDNet用于场景变化检测：Transformer编码器+相关体融合+三门GRU递归解码+卷积-插值上采样；在四个基准上优于现有方法，并在视角偏差下具鲁棒性；分割预训练与融合设计有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SCD方法存在三大问题：1) 忽视不同层级特征的重要性差异；2) 解码器多为单步，限制细化能力；3) 对编码器预训练策略缺少系统性研究。为提升变化掩码精细度、稳健性与泛化性，需要新的架构与训练策略。

Method: 提出TERDNet：1) Transformer编码器提取多层级表示；2) 特征融合模块将相关体(correlation volumes)与多尺度特征融合；3) 采用带三门设计的递归GRU解码器进行多步迭代细化；4) 结合卷积与插值的上采样以恢复细粒度分辨率；并进行分割任务预训练与消融分析、鲁棒性测试（视角不对齐）。

Result: 在四个公开基准上整体性能优于既有方法，生成更准确、细致的变化掩码；消融显示分割预训练与融合模块显著贡献；在视角偏差测试中表现稳健，适用于机器人真实场景。

Conclusion: TERDNet通过Transformer编码器+递归解码与有效融合，上采样策略协同，实现SCD的精细与稳健检测；实验与消融验证其优势与实践潜力，特别是在视角不对齐环境下。

Abstract: In this work, we address the challenge of Scene Change Detection (SCD), where the goal is to identify variations between two images of the same location captured at different times. Existing SCD models often overlook the varying importance of features across layers, employ single-step decoders that confine refinement, and provide limited insight into encoder pretraining strategies. We propose TERDNet, a Transformer Encoder-Recurrent Decoder Network designed to overcome these limitations. TERDNet consists of a transformer-based encoder that extracts multi-level representations, a feature fusion module that integrates correlation volumes with these features, a recurrent 3-gate-GRU decoder that performs iterative refinement, and a combined convolution-interpolation upsampler that restores fine-grained resolution. Extensive experiments on four public benchmarks show that TERDNet consistently outperforms prior approaches and produces more accurate and detailed change masks. Ablation studies confirm the benefit of segmentation-based pretraining and the effectiveness of our fusion design. In addition, robustness tests under viewpoint misalignment confirm TERDNet's potential for deployment in real-world robotic systems, where reliable perception is critical. Our code is available at https://github.com/AutoCompSysLab/TERDNet.

</details>


### [79] [RelWitness: Open-Vocabulary 3D Scene Graph Generation with Visual-Geometric Relation Witnesses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20823)
*Minh Anh Nguyen,Quang Huy Tran,Bao Ngoc Le,Tuan Kiet Pham,Sui Yang Guang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RelWitness提出在开放词汇3D场景图生成中，用“关系见证”将视觉/几何可观测证据与谓词关系对齐，以在不完整标注下更可靠学习；通过见证验证与PU学习，提升未见关系识别、降低幻觉与冗余。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3D场景图中的关系标注稀疏且选择性强，导致大量真实关系未被标注，传统监督会把缺失当负例，限制开放词汇泛化；需要一种利用可观测几何与多视图线索来“证明”关系、纠正监督偏差的方法。

Method: 引入“关系见证”的概念，并为不同关系定义可观测几何/时空条件（接触+竖直次序、包围、距离、朝向、跨视角稳定性）。从多源信号（RGB、深度、重建3D、角色敏感文本、对象先验空视图、多视一致）构建见证记录；用见证验证器将未标注候选划为缺失正例、可靠负例或不确定；基于见证引导的PU目标训练模型，避免把所有缺失当负；推理阶段采用见证一致解码；并提出RGB-D缺失关系审计协议与开放词汇数据划分。

Result: 在3DSSG/3RScan与ScanNet派生的开放词汇划分上的“规划性”实验显示：未见关系识别提升、见证精度更高、关系幻觉更少、冗余短语减少（作者声明数值为占位，提交前需以复现实测替换）。

Conclusion: 通过将可观测几何/多视线索显式建模为关系见证，并结合见证驱动的PU学习与解码，能在不完整监督下改进开放词汇3D场景图的关系检测与表述，同时提供可审计性；需后续以真实复现实验验证数值。

Abstract: Open-vocabulary 3D scene graph generation seeks to describe object instances and their relations with flexible natural-language predicates. The central difficulty is not only vocabulary expansion, but supervision reliability: relation annotations in 3D scene graph datasets are selective, and many valid object-pair relations are unannotated. We propose RelWitness, a framework for open-vocabulary 3D scene graph generation from posed RGB-D sequences under incomplete relation supervision. The key concept is a relation witness: a concrete visual-geometric cue that makes a relation observable in the captured scene. Support relations require contact and vertical ordering; containment requires enclosure; proximity requires metric closeness; orientation requires facing direction; and stable relations should persist across views where both objects are visible. RelWitness constructs relation witness records from RGB views, depth maps, reconstructed 3D geometry, role-sensitive text, object-prior null views, and multi-view consistency. A visual-geometric witness verifier assigns unannotated relation candidates to verified missing positives, reliable negatives, or uncertain unlabeled cases. A witness-guided positive-unlabeled objective then learns from incomplete annotations without turning every missing label into a negative. We further introduce witness-consistent decoding and an RGB-D missing-relation audit protocol. Simulated manuscript-planning experiments on 3DSSG/3RScan and ScanNet-derived open-vocabulary splits show the intended behavior: improved unseen-relation recognition, higher witness precision, lower hallucination, and reduced redundant relation phrases. All numerical results are planning values and must be replaced by reproduced measurements before submission

### [80] [HyDAR-Pano3D: A Hybrid Disentangled Anatomical Recovery Framework for Panoramic-to-3D Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20827)
*Yaoyao Yue,Jérôme Schmid,Xiaoshuang Li,Eduardo Delamare,Jinman Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HyDAR-Pano3D 将“从全景片重建CBCT”的难题拆为两步：先重建标准化的解剖基准体，再用受限形变场恢复个体差异，从而显著提升清晰度与解剖一致性，并支持下游临床分割。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接从2D全景片回归3D CBCT需同时学习共性解剖与个体变异，导致问题高度不适定、易过度平滑和边界模糊。需要一种解耦策略，将“共性结构恢复”和“个体形态还原”分离。

Method: 两阶段解耦重建：Stage 1 用双编码网络融合放射学特征与由SAM得到的语义先验，重建牙弓归一化的规范（canonical）体积；Stage 2 以解剖恢复网络预测受先验约束的结构化形变场，将规范体映射回原生空间，恢复个体形态。

Result: 在三大数据集上显著优于基线（p<0.05），达成PSNR 25.76 dB、SSIM 85.70%、整体解剖Dice 83.83%；用于下游分割：全牙Dice 82.4%、下牙槽管Dice 72.2%。

Conclusion: 将PR→CBCT视作“解剖恢复+个体形变”两步，可缓解2D→3D不适定性，获得更清晰、结构保真的重建，并在无CBCT时实现可靠的解剖感知评估。

Abstract: Panoramic radiograph (PR) is fundamentally used in routine dental care, but it inherently provides only a two-dimensional (2D) projection of complex three-dimensional (3D) craniofacial anatomy. Most existing learning-based methods attempt to computationally recover this 3D information by directly regressing native cone-beam computed tomography (CBCT) volumes from PR. However, this direct mapping requires the model to simultaneously learn common anatomical structures and patient-specific morphological variations. This entangled formulation makes the ill-posed 2D-to-3D inverse problem highly ambiguous, often producing over-smoothed reconstructions with blurred anatomical boundaries. To address this, we propose HyDAR-Pano3D, a two-stage framework that reformulates PR-to-CBCT reconstruction as a disentangled anatomical recovery problem. In Stage 1, a dual-encoder network integrates radiographic features with SAM-derived semantic priors to reconstruct an arch-normalized canonical volume. In Stage 2, an Anatomical Restoration Network predicts a prior-constrained structured deformation field to map this canonical volume back to the native space, restoring individual morphological variations. Experiments on three large-scale datasets show that HyDAR-Pano3D significantly outperforms baseline methods ($p < 0.05$), achieving a 25.76 dB PSNR, 85.70\% SSIM, and an 83.83\% overall anatomical Dice score. The synthesized volumes successfully support downstream segmentation of whole teeth (82.4\% Dice) and the inferior alveolar canal (72.2\% Dice), demonstrating that our disentangled approach preserves clinically relevant structures to enable robust anatomy-aware assessment when CBCT data is unavailable.

### [81] [ArchSIBench: Benchmarking the Architectural Spatial Intelligence of Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20837)
*Qirui Shen,Wenda Wang,Jiachen Lu,Zilong Huang,Jin Bai,Lei He,Hongxuan Chen,Weixin Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ArchSIBench：一个衡量建筑空间智能的多维基准，含5大维度17子任务、3000问答；评测多种VLM，发现与人类（尤其受过建筑训练者）仍有显著差距，尤其在空间变换与配置推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLM空间评测多停留在基础技能（朝向、距离、计数），忽视对建筑空间高级认知（布局、流线、功能分区）。为系统衡量并推动VLM在建筑空间理解与推理方面的能力，需要一个跨学科、细粒度的标准化基准。

Method: 从建筑学、认知科学与心理学视角设计覆盖感知、推理、导航、变换、配置五个维度的17个细粒度子任务；由具建筑背景的专家精标3000个问答对；用该基准系统评测多种VLM，与人类基线（有/无建筑训练）比较维度化表现。

Result: 多数VLM与人类基线差异明显，且在不同能力维度上波动较大；部分SOTA模型可接近无建筑训练的人类评审水平，但与受过建筑训练的人类相比仍存在明显差距，尤其在空间变换与配置推理上表现不足。

Conclusion: ArchSIBench为衡量与推进VLM的建筑空间智能提供了系统资源与洞见；尽管某些模型已接近非专业人类水平，但要达到专业建筑认知仍需改进，特别是空间变换和配置层面的能力。

Abstract: Architectural spatial intelligence, the ability to recognize and infer architectural space, is fundamental to tasks such as robot navigation, embodied interaction, and 3D scene understanding and generation. Although extensive research has evaluated the basic spatial skills of Vision-Language Models (VLMs) such as relative orientation, distance comparison, and object counting, these tasks cover only the most elementary levels of spatial cognition and largely overlook higher-level cognition of architectural space, including layout understanding, circulation patterns, and functional zoning. In this work, we present ArchSIBench, a Benchmark for Architectural Spatial Intelligence based on the perspectives from architecture, cognitive science, and psychology. ArchSIBench covers five core dimensions: perception, reasoning, navigation, transformation, and configuration, comprising 17 fine-grained subtasks. Through careful manual annotation by experts with architectural backgrounds, we construct 3,000 question-answer pairs to enable comprehensive evaluation of architectural spatial intelligence. Based on ArchSIBench, we evaluate various VLMs and find that the architectural spatial intelligence of most models shows significant differences from human baselines; additionally, models exhibit substantial variability across capability dimensions. Some state-of-the-art models can approach the level of human evaluators without architectural training. However, a clear gap remains compared to human evaluators with architectural training, particularly in spatial transformation and configuration reasoning. We believe that ArchSIBench will provide important insights and systematic resources for measuring and advancing the architectural spatial intelligence of VLMs. The dataset and code are available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/ArchSIBench/ArchSIBench.

</details>

Although video understanding has achieved plausible improvement these years, most works focus on instance-level recognition, which is not sufficient for learning the representation of the high-level semantic information of videos. Therefore, we further establish two tasks: topic recognition and video-text retrieval on USV. We propose two unified and effective baseline methods Multi-Modality Fusion Network (MMF-Net) and Video-Text Contrastive Learning (VTCL), to tackle the topic recognition task and video-text retrieval respectively, and carry out comprehensive benchmarks to facilitate future research. Our project page is https://usvdataset.github.io.

### [83] [Activation-Free Backbones for Image Recognition: Polynomial Alternatives within MetaFormer-Style Vision Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20839)
*Jeffrey Wang,Jonathan Gregory,Grigorios G. Chrysos*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出在MetaFormer风格视觉骨干中，用多项式模块替代常见的点式激活与softmax，仍可达到或超越原有性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主流视觉网络依赖ReLU/GELU与softmax提供非线性，但这些可能并非必要；若能去激活并以更简单的多项式机制取得同等或更好效果，可带来更稳健、更高效且更可解释的网络。

Method: 为三类核心算子（MLP、卷积、注意力）构造无激活的多项式替代：用Hadamard逐元素乘法堆叠实现多项式非线性，替换点式激活和softmax；将这些模块嵌入MetaFormer框架形成PolyNeXt系列，并在各尺度评测。

Result: 在ImageNet分类、ADE20K语义分割及分布外鲁棒性上，PolyNeXt与或超过常规模型；相较既有多项式网络，以更低算力取得显著更好表现。

Conclusion: 点式激活与softmax并非MetaFormer类视觉骨干的必要非线性来源；标准模块的多项式变体简单高效，能优于复杂定制多项式架构，具备实用价值。

Abstract: Modern vision backbones treat pointwise activations (e.g., ReLU, GELU) and exponential softmax as essential sources of nonlinearity, but we demonstrate they are not required within MetaFormer-style vision backbones. We design activation-free polynomial alternatives for three core primitives (MLPs, convolutions, and attention), where Hadamard products replace standard nonlinearities to yield polynomial functions of the input. These modules integrate seamlessly into existing architectures: instantiated within MetaFormer, a modular framework for vision backbones, our PolyNeXt models match or exceed activation-based counterparts across model scales on ImageNet classification, ADE20K semantic segmentation, and out-of-distribution robustness. We also substantially outperform prior polynomial networks at reduced computational cost, showing that polynomial variants of standard modules beat complex custom architectures.

### [85] [HDMoE: A Hierarchical Decoupling-Fusion Mixture-of-Experts Framework for Multimodal Cancer Survival Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20891)
*Huayi Wang,Haochao Ying,Yuyang Xu,Qiyao Zheng,jun wang,Cheng Zhang,Ying Sun,Jian Wu*

Method: 提出HDMoE框架：包含两级MoE与两个随机特征重组（RFR）模块。第一级MoE用共享专家与路由专家在各模态内去冗余并提取细粒度特异特征；随后RFR对模态内特征做精细融合。第二级MoE在跨模态层面进行细粒度解耦以突出互补性；再用另一RFR对跨模态特征做精细融合，提升模态间关系捕获能力。

Abstract: Multimodal survival prediction, a crucial yet challenging task, demands the integration of multimodal medical data (\eg Whole Slide Images (WSIs) and Genomic Profiles) to achieve accurate prognostic modeling. Given the inherent heterogeneity across modalities, the feature decoupling-fusion paradigm has emerged as a dominant approach. However, these methods have the following shortcomings: (1) fail to reduce the redundant information of modality features before decoupling, which negatively affects the feature decoupling and fusion effect;(2) lack the ability to model the fine-grained relationships of the features and capture the local information interactions between intra- and inter-modality features. To address these issues, we propose a \underline{H}ierarchical \underline{D}ecoupling-Fusion \underline{M}ixture-\underline{o}f-\underline{E}xperts (HDMoE) framework with two levels of MoE and \underline{R}andom \underline{F}eature \underline{R}eorganization (RFR) modules.In the first-level MoE, shared experts and routed experts are employed to remove redundant information and extract fine-grained specific features within each modality, while the second-level MoE facilitates fine-grained inter-modality feature decoupling. Besides, we design two RFR modules following each level of MoE to finely fuse intra- and inter-modality features, which can help the model capture more fine-grained relationships between modalities. Extensive experimental results on our private Liver Cancer (LC) and three TCGA public datasets confirm the effectiveness of our proposed method. Codes are available at https://github.com/ZJUMAI/HDMoE.

Furthermore, we optimized the training pipeline with a hard sample-aware joint loss. Our framework provides an efficient, deployment-oriented solution for real-world agricultural visual sorting and quality inspection tasks.

### [87] [VISTA: Technical Report for the Ego4D Short-Term Object Interaction Anticipation at EgoVis 2026](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20901)
*Qiaohui Chu,Haoyu Zhang,Yisen Feng,Meng Liu,Weili Guan,Dongmei Jiang,Liqiang Nie*

Main category: cs.CV

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We propose VISTA, a V-JEPA Integrated StillFast Temporal Anticipator for the Ego4D Short-Term Object Interaction Anticipation (STA) Challenge at EgoVis 2026. Given an egocentric video timestamp, the task requires anticipating the next human-object interaction, including the future active object's bounding box, noun category, verb category, time-to-contact, and confidence score. VISTA follows a StillFast-style design that combines object-centric spatial detection with short-horizon temporal context. Specifically, a COCO-pretrained Faster R-CNN ResNet-50 FPN detector generates object proposals from the last observed high-resolution frame, while a frozen V-JEPA 2.1 temporal branch extracts clip-level egocentric context from the observed video. The temporal representation is injected into the detection pathway through feature modulation and ROI-level context fusion. The fused proposal features are then passed to multi-head STA predictors for box refinement, noun classification, verb classification, time-to-contact regression, and interaction confidence estimation. For the final submission, we further ensemble complementary predictions to improve robustness. Experimental results on the official challenge server show that VISTA achieves first place in the EgoVis 2026 Ego4D STA Challenge. Our code will be released at https://github.com/CorrineQiu/VISTA.

Inspired by the representation learning and future prediction ability of V-JEPA 2.1, JFAA uses a frozen encoder and predictor to extract observed context features and near-future latent tokens. A lightweight attentive probe is then trained to predict verb, noun, and action logits with separate task queries. To improve robustness, we further build a field-aware ensemble over selected epoch-level predictions, allowing each output field to benefit from its most reliable candidates. Experimental results on the official challenge server show that JFAA achieves first place in the EgoVis 2026 EK-100 Action Anticipation Challenge.
